MUNICIPAL ADMINISTRATION AND WATER SUPPLY DEPARTMENT
PROPOSED FOR DELIMITATION OF CERTAIN DIVISIONS UNDER
THE COIMBATORE CITY MUNICIPAL CORPORATION ACT.
[Üóê£¬í (G¬ô) â‡ 114, ïèó£†C G˜õ£è‹ ñŸÁ‹ °®c˜ õöƒè™ («î˜î™) ¶¬ø,

No. II(2)/MAWS/383(b-1)/2011.
Under  sub-section (1) of section 51 of the Coimbatore City Municipal Corporation Act,1981 (Tamil Nadu Act
25 of 1981) and in supersession of all previous notifications issued on the above subject, the Governor of
Tamil Nadu hereby divides the City of Coimbatore into one hundred territorial divisions for the purpose of election
of one hundred councillors and hereby fixes the boundaries of the said one hundred divisions, as described in the
Schedule below:—
2. This delimitation shall take effect from the next ordinary elections to the Council of Municipal Corporation of
Coimbatore.

91
PROPOSAL FOR DELIMITATION OF CERTAIN DIVISIONS UNDER THE ERODE CITY MUNICIPAL 
CORPORATION ACT. 
 
[Üóê£¬í (G¬ô) â‡ 115, ïèó£†C G˜õ£è‹ ñŸÁ‹ °®c˜ õöƒè™ («î˜î™) ¶¬ø,  
25 Ýèv´ 2011.] 
 
No. II(2)/MAWS/383(b-2)/2011. 
Under sub-section (1) of section 51 of the Coimbatore City Municipal Corporation Act,1981 (Tamil Nadu Act 25 of 
1981) read with section 8 of the Erode City Municipal Corporation Act,2008 (Tamil Nadu Act 8 of 2008) and in 
supersession of all previous notifications issued on the above subject, the Governor of Tamil Nadu here by divides 
the City of Erode into sixty territorial divisions for the purpose of election of sixty councillors and hereby fixes the 
boundaries of the said sixty divisions, as described in the Schedule below. 
2. This delimitation shall take effect from the next ordinary elections to the Council of Municipal Corporation of 
Erode.
